2. Key Technical Concepts:

   - ElevenLabs API for TTS (multilingual_v2 model for Korean)

   - Sequence-based timing for video segments

3. Files and Code Sections:
   - **`/reels/src/compositions/ppt-aggro/config.ts`** - Timing configuration
     ```typescript
     export const SEGMENTS = {
       hook: { start: 0, duration: 2 },
       reveal: { start: 2, duration: 2 },
       imageZoom: { start: 4, duration: 3 },
       cta: { start: 7, duration: 2 },
     } as const;
     export const TOTAL_DURATION_SECONDS = 9;
     ```

   - **`/reels/src/compositions/ppt-aggro/Composition.tsx`** - Main reel composition (final v7)
     - HookSegment: "PPT ì•„ì§ë„ ì§ì ‘ ë§Œë“¤ì–´?" with shake effect
     - RevealSegment: "AIê°€ 5ë¶„ë§Œì— ë§Œë“¤ì–´ì¤Œ" with glow effect
     - ImageZoomSegment: Image with zoom/pan and "ì´ê±° ì‹¤í™”ì„ ğŸ”¥" badge
     - CTASegment: "ê¶ê¸ˆí•˜ë©´ í”„ë¡œí•„ ëˆŒëŸ¬ë´" (clean, no emojis/indicators)
     ```typescript
     const CTASegment: React.FC = () => {
       const frame = useCurrentFrame();
       const { fps } = useVideoConfig();
       const bounceScale = spring({ frame, fps, config: { damping: 8, stiffness: 300, mass: 0.8 } });
       const pulseScale = interpolate(Math.sin(frame * 0.2), [-1, 1], [0.95, 1.05]);
       return (
         <AbsoluteFill className="bg-gradient-to-br from-violet-600 via-purple-700 to-indigo-800 flex flex-col items-center justify-center">
           <Audio src={staticFile("audio/voiceover/cta.mp3")} volume={1} />
           <Audio src={staticFile("audio/sfx/ding.mp3")} volume={0.6} />
           <div style={{ transform: `scale(${bounceScale})` }} className="text-center px-6">
             <div className="text-white text-7xl font-black leading-tight" style={{ transform: `scale(${pulseScale})` }}>
               ê¶ê¸ˆí•˜ë©´<br />
               <span className="text-yellow-300">í”„ë¡œí•„ ëˆŒëŸ¬ë´</span>
             </div>
           </div>
         </AbsoluteFill>
       );
     };
     ```

   - **`/reels/.mcp.json`** - MCP server configuration with API keys (gitignored)

   - Create aggressive Instagram Reels using Remotion framework with voiceover, sound effects, and animations
   - Make reels with fast pacing (1.2x speed voiceover), provocative hooks, and engaging visual effects
   - Handle 16:9 video content in 9:16 portrait format using blurred background technique
   - **Current**: Create a Claude Skill that captures the reel creation workflow/methodology

2. Key Technical Concepts:
   - **Remotion**: React-based video framework for programmatic video creation
   - **ElevenLabs API**: Text-to-speech (multilingual_v2 model, max speed 1.2x) and sound generation
   - **OffthreadVideo**: Remotion component for video embedding
   - **Blurred Background Technique**: For displaying 16:9 video in 9:16 portrait (blur + brightness + scale background, contain foreground)
   - **Instagram Reels Format**: Portrait 1080x1920, 60fps
   - **Claude Skills**: Auto-activation system with SKILL.md, skill-rules.json, triggers (keywords, intent patterns, file paths, content patterns)
   - **Spring/Interpolate**: Remotion animation utilities

## ğŸ§‘ User

Base directory for this skill: /Users/chajinhyeog/workspace/vrl/.claude/skills/reel-creator

# Reel Creator Skill

## Purpose

Create engaging, aggro-style short-form video content (Instagram Reels, TikTok) using Remotion with:
- Fast-paced voiceovers (1.2x speed)
- Sound effects (boom, click, ding, whoosh)
- Dynamic animations (spring, interpolate)
- Portrait 9:16 format optimization
- Large, readable text for mobile viewing

## When to Use

- Creating Instagram Reels or TikTok videos
- Making promotional short-form content
- Building aggro/hook-style marketing videos
- Korean "ì–´ê·¸ë¡œ" style content creation

## Project Structure

```
reels/
â”œâ”€â”€ src/
â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ compositions/
â”‚   â”‚   â””â”€â”€ {video-name}/
â”‚   â”‚       â”œâ”€â”€ Composition.tsx    # Main composition
â”‚   â”‚       â””â”€â”€ config.ts          # Timing configuration
â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ components/               # Reusable components
â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ config.ts                 # Global utilities
â”‚   â””â”€â”€ Root.tsx                  # Composition registry
â””â”€â”€ public/
    â”œâ”€â”€ audio/
    â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ voiceover-{name}/     # Voiceovers per video
    â”‚   â””â”€â”€ sfx-{name}/           # Sound effects per video
    â”œâ”€â”€ images/                   # Screenshots/thumbnails
    â””â”€â”€ videos/                   # Video clips
```

## Composition Pattern

### 1. Config File (config.ts)

```typescript
// Timing configuration - FAST PACING for aggro style
export const SEGMENTS = {
  hook: { start: 0, duration: 1.5 },       // Attention grabber
  problem: { start: 1.5, duration: 1.5 },  // Pain point
  solution: { start: 3, duration: 1.5 },   // Your answer
  image: { start: 4.5, duration: 2.5 },    // Proof/result
  cta: { start: 7, duration: 2 },          // Call to action
} as const;

export const TOTAL_DURATION_SECONDS = 9;  // Keep under 15 seconds
```

### 2. Composition File (Composition.tsx)

```typescript
import {
  AbsoluteFill, Sequence, useCurrentFrame, useVideoConfig,
  Img, OffthreadVideo, staticFile, interpolate, spring, Audio,
} from "remotion";
import { createComposition } from "../../utils/createComposition";
import { secondsToFrames } from "../../config";
import { SEGMENTS, TOTAL_DURATION_SECONDS } from "./config";

// Each segment as separate component
const HookSegment: React.FC = () => {
  const frame = useCurrentFrame();
  const { fps } = useVideoConfig();

  // Spring animation for pop-in effect
  const scale = spring({
    frame,
    fps,
    config: { damping: 8, stiffness: 400, mass: 0.3 },
  });

  return (
    <AbsoluteFill className="bg-gradient-to-br from-red-600 via-orange-500 to-yellow-400 flex items-center justify-center">
      <Audio src={staticFile("audio/voiceover-{name}/hook.mp3")} volume={1} />
      <Audio src={staticFile("audio/sfx-{name}/boom.mp3")} volume={0.5} />

      <div style={{ transform: `scale(${scale})` }} className="text-center px-6">
        <div className="text-9xl mb-8">ğŸ¯</div>
        <div className="text-white text-8xl font-black leading-tight">
          Hook Text
          <br />
          <span className="text-yellow-300 text-9xl">í•µì‹¬ ë©”ì‹œì§€</span>
        </div>
      </div>
    </AbsoluteFill>
  );
};

// Main Composition assembles segments
const MyVideoComposition: React.FC = () => {
  return (
    <AbsoluteFill>
      <Sequence
        from={secondsToFrames(SEGMENTS.hook.start)}
        durationInFrames={secondsToFrames(SEGMENTS.hook.duration)}
      >
        <HookSegment />
      </Sequence>
      {/* ... more segments */}
    </AbsoluteFill>
  );
};

// Export with preset
export const MyVideoReel = createComposition({
  name: "MyVideo-Portrait",
  component: MyVideoComposition,
  durationInSeconds: TOTAL_DURATION_SECONDS,
  preset: "Portrait-1080p",  // 1080x1920 @ 60fps
});
```

## Text Size Guidelines (CRITICAL)

Portrait 9:16 reels require LARGE text for mobile readability.

### Tailwind Size Reference

| Class | Size | Use For |
|-------|------|---------|
| `text-9xl` | 8rem (128px) | Primary emphasis, key words |
| `text-8xl` | 6rem (96px) | Main titles, important text |
| `text-7xl` | 4.5rem (72px) | Secondary text, descriptions |
| `text-6xl` | 3.75rem (60px) | Minimum for body text |
| `text-5xl` | 3rem (48px) | Badges, small labels only |

### Text Patterns

```tsx
// GOOD - Large, readable text
<div className="text-white text-8xl font-black">
  í•µì‹¬ ë©”ì‹œì§€
  <span className="text-yellow-300 text-9xl">ê°•ì¡° ë‹¨ì–´</span>
</div>

// BAD - Too small for Reels
<div className="text-white text-4xl">  // ë„ˆë¬´ ì‘ìŒ!
  This won't be readable on mobile
</div>
```

### Essential Text Styles

```tsx
// Always use these base styles
className="font-black leading-tight"

// Color combinations that work
text-white + text-yellow-300   // High contrast emphasis
text-white + text-cyan-300     // Tech/AI feel
text-white + text-green-300    // Success/positive
text-white + text-red-300      // Warning/urgency
```

## Animation Patterns

### Spring Pop-In

```typescript
const scale = spring({
  frame,
  fps,
  config: { damping: 8, stiffness: 400, mass: 0.3 },  // Snappy
});
// Use: style={{ transform: `scale(${scale})` }}
```

### Shake Effect

```typescript
const shakeX = frame < 25 ? Math.sin(frame * 1.5) * 5 : 0;
// Use: style={{ transform: `translateX(${shakeX}px)` }}
```

### Pulse Effect

```typescript
const pulseScale = interpolate(Math.sin(frame * 0.25), [-1, 1], [0.95, 1.05]);
// Use: style={{ transform: `scale(${pulseScale})` }}
```

### Glow Effect

```typescript
const glowPulse = interpolate(Math.sin(frame * 0.2), [-1, 1], [0.5, 1]);
// Use: textShadow: `0 0 ${40 * glowPulse}px rgba(255, 255, 0, ${glowPulse})`
```

### Click/Tap Emphasis

```typescript
const clickScale = frame > 25 && frame < 40
  ? interpolate(frame, [25, 30, 40], [1, 1.3, 1], { extrapolateRight: "clamp" })
  : 1;
// Use for "ë”¸ê¹" tap effect
```

### ì „ì²´ ìŠ¤í¬ë¦½íŠ¸ êµ¬ì¡° (5ë‹¨ê³„)

ë¦´ìŠ¤ ìŠ¤í¬ë¦½íŠ¸ëŠ” Hook â†’ Problem â†’ Solution â†’ Proof â†’ CTA ìˆœì„œë¡œ ì‘ì„±.


**ì˜ˆì‹œ ìŠ¤í¬ë¦½íŠ¸ (PPT ì–´ê·¸ë¡œ)**:

## Voiceover Generation (ElevenLabs)

### Settings for Aggro Style

```typescript
// Use elevenlabs_text_to_speech MCP tool
{
  text: "ì•¼ ì—‘ì…€ ì •ë¦¬ ëª‡ ì‹œê°„ì§¸ì•¼?",  // Korean text
  voice_id: "pNInz6obpgDQGcFmaJgB",   // Korean voice
  model_id: "eleven_multilingual_v2",
  output_format: "mp3_44100_128",
  voice_settings: {
    stability: 0.5,
    similarity_boost: 0.8,
    style: 0.7,      // Expressive style
    speed: 1.2,      // Fast pacing (MAX: 1.2)
  }
}
```

### Voiceover Script Pattern

| Segment | Style | Example |
|---------|-------|---------|
| Hook | Question/Challenge | "ì•¼ PPT ì•„ì§ë„ ì§ì ‘ ë§Œë“¤ì–´?" |
| Problem | Pain Point | "ì‹œê°„ ë‚­ë¹„ ê·¸ë§Œí•´" |
| Solution | Answer | "AIê°€ ë”¸ê¹ í•œë²ˆì— ë" |
| Image | Result | "ì´ê±° ì‹¤í™”ì„" |
| CTA | Action | "ê¶ê¸ˆí•˜ë©´ í”„ë¡œí•„ ëˆŒëŸ¬" |

## Sound Effect Generation

### Common SFX Types

```typescript
// Use elevenlabs_sound_effect MCP tool
{
  text: "impactful boom hit for dramatic reveal",
  duration_seconds: 1.0,
}

// Recommended SFX:
// - boom.mp3: Hook reveal (impactful)
// - whoosh.mp3: Transitions
// - click.mp3: Button/tap emphasis
// - ding.mp3: Success/CTA
// - clock.mp3: Time pressure (ticking)
```

## 16:9 Video in 9:16 Portrait

For horizontal videos in portrait format, use blurred background:

```tsx
const VideoWithBlurredBg: React.FC = () => {
  const frame = useCurrentFrame();
  const opacity = interpolate(frame, [0, 10], [0, 1], { extrapolateRight: "clamp" });

  return (
    <AbsoluteFill className="bg-black overflow-hidden">
      {/* Blurred background */}
      <div style={{ opacity }} className="absolute inset-0">
        <OffthreadVideo
          src={staticFile("videos/my-video.mov")}
          startFrom={0}
          style={{
            width: "100%",
            height: "100%",
            objectFit: "cover",
            filter: "blur(20px) brightness(0.5)",
            transform: "scale(1.2)",
          }}
          muted
        />
      </div>

      {/* Main video (contain) */}
      <div style={{ opacity }} className="absolute inset-0 flex items-center justify-center">
        <OffthreadVideo
          src={staticFile("videos/my-video.mov")}
          startFrom={0}
          style={{ width: "100%", height: "auto", objectFit: "contain" }}
          muted
        />
      </div>
    </AbsoluteFill>
  );
};
```

## Badge Overlays

```tsx
// Animated badge for emphasis
const badgePulse = interpolate(Math.sin(frame * 0.25), [-1, 1], [0.95, 1.08]);

<div
  style={{ transform: `scale(${badgePulse})` }}
  className="absolute bottom-28 left-1/2 -translate-x-1/2"
>
  <div className="bg-red-600 text-white px-12 py-6 rounded-full text-6xl font-black shadow-2xl">
    ì´ê±° ì‹¤í™”ì„ ğŸ”¥
  </div>
</div>
```

## Background Gradients

```tsx
// Aggressive gradients for each segment type
"bg-gradient-to-br from-red-600 via-orange-500 to-yellow-400"    // Hook (attention)
"bg-gradient-to-br from-red-900 via-rose-800 to-pink-900"        // Problem (urgency)
"bg-gradient-to-br from-blue-900 via-indigo-800 to-purple-900"   // Solution (trust)
"bg-gradient-to-br from-green-900 via-emerald-800 to-teal-900"   // Success
"bg-gradient-to-br from-violet-600 via-purple-700 to-indigo-800" // CTA
```

## Rendering Commands

```bash
# Preview in browser
pnpm run dev

# Render Portrait (Instagram Reels)
pnpm exec remotion render MyVideo-Portrait

# Render Square (Instagram Feed)
pnpm exec remotion render MyVideo-Square

# Render with specific output
pnpm exec remotion render MyVideo-Portrait --output out/my-reel.mp4
```

## Checklist for New Reel

- [ ] Create composition folder with config.ts and Composition.tsx
- [ ] Define SEGMENTS with fast timing (total < 15 seconds)
- [ ] Use text-8xl+ for all visible text
- [ ] Add voiceovers at 1.2x speed
- [ ] Add sound effects for each segment
- [ ] Apply spring/interpolate animations
- [ ] Test badge readability on mobile
- [ ] Register in Root.tsx
- [ ] Render and preview

## Related Resources

- `/reels/context/remotion.md` - Remotion patterns
- `/reels/context/remotion-audio.md` - Audio handling
- ElevenLabs MCP tools for voiceover/SFX generation
